### SEO Best Practices

- Write compelling meta descriptions (120-155 characters)
- Use a single H1 tag per page that describes the main topic
- Structure content with proper heading hierarchy (H1 â†’ H2 â†’ H3)
- Add descriptive alt text to all images
- Implement structured data (JSON-LD) for rich search results

- Use HTTPS and ensure canonical URLs are set
